<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="34eb17db783b4bfc89d6af11f1a67a1c"><span data-offset-key="34eb17db783b4bfc89d6af11f1a67a1c:0">The goal of this book is to provide an Informatics-oriented introduction to programming. The primary difference between a computer science approach and the Informatics approach taken in this book is a greater focus on using Python to solve data analysis problems common in the world of Informatics.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b6a89ecaa28648f9bf4f20737a4fe5fc"><span data-offset-key="b6a89ecaa28648f9bf4f20737a4fe5fc:0">The sample code and data files for the book is here: </span></span><a href="https://www.py4e.com/code3/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="57bb2922b59f41a5aad171e001a41e30"><span data-offset-key="57bb2922b59f41a5aad171e001a41e30:0">Code Samples</span></span></a><span data-key="d7d4eba8299d49aab2ca46059354dd69"><span data-offset-key="d7d4eba8299d49aab2ca46059354dd69:0">.</span></span></span>
